Operating System Configuration
==============================

Make configuration changes related to the operating system or a common feature of the operating system that result in system hardening against techniques.

ID:M0928

Security Controls:IEC 62443-3-3:2013 - SR 7.7, IEC 62443-4-2:2019 - CR 7.7, NIST SP 800-53 Rev. 5 - CM-7

Version:1.0

Created:06 June 2019

Last Modified:19 September 2023

[Version Permalink](https://attack.mitre.org/versions/v15/mitigations/M0928/)

**ATT&CK********Navigator Layers**

**Techniques Addressed by Mitigation**
--------------------------------------

**Domain**

**ID**

**Name**

**Use**

ICS

[T0895](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0895)

[Autorun Image](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0895)

Configure operating systems to disable the autorun of any specific file types or drives.

ICS

[T0847](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0847)

[Replication Through Removable Media](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0847)

Harden the system through operating system controls to prevent the known or unknown use of malicious removable media.

Operational Information Confidentiality
=======================================

Deploy mechanisms to protect the confidentiality of information related to operational processes, facility locations, device configurations, programs, or databases that may have information that can be used to infer organizational trade-secrets, recipes, and other intellectual property (IP).

ID:M0809

Security Controls:IEC 62443-3-3:2013 - SR 4.1, IEC 62443-4-2:2019 - CR 4.1

Version:1.0

Created:06 June 2019

Last Modified:30 March 2023

[Version Permalink](https://attack.mitre.org/versions/v15/mitigations/M0809/)

**ATT&CK********Navigator Layers**

**Techniques Addressed by Mitigation**
--------------------------------------

**Domain**

**ID**

**Name**

**Use**

ICS

[T0882](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0882)

[Theft of Operational Information](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0882)

Example mitigations could include minimizing its distribution/storage or obfuscating the information (e.g., facility coverterms, codenames). In many cases this information may be necessary to support critical engineering, maintenance, or operational functions, therefore, it may not be feasible to implement.

Out-of-Band Communications Channel
==================================

Have alternative methods to support communication requirements during communication failures and data integrity attacks.[\[1\]](https://nvlpubs.nist.gov/nistpubs/SpecialPublications/NIST.SP.800-53r4.pdf)[\[2\]](https://www.darpa.mil/program/rapid-attack-detection-isolation-and-characterization-systems)

ID:M0810

Security Controls:NIST SP 800-53 Rev. 5 - SC-37

Version:1.0

Created:06 June 2019

Last Modified:19 September 2023

[Version Permalink](https://attack.mitre.org/versions/v15/mitigations/M0810/)

**ATT&CK********Navigator Layers**

**Techniques Addressed by Mitigation**
--------------------------------------

**Domain**

**ID**

**Name**

**Use**

ICS

[T0830](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0830)

[Adversary-in-the-Middle](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0830)

Utilize out-of-band communication to validate the integrity of data from the primary channel.

ICS

[T0878](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0878)

[Alarm Suppression](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0878)

Provide an alternative method for alarms to be reported in the event of a communication failure.

ICS

[T0803](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0803)

[Block Command Message](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0803)

Provide an alternative method for sending critical commands message to outstations, this could include using radio/cell communication to send messages to a field technician that physically performs the control function.

ICS

[T0804](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0804)

[Block Reporting Message](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0804)

Provide an alternative method for sending critical report messages to operators, this could include using radio/cell communication to obtain messages from field technicians that can locally obtain telemetry and status data.

ICS

[T0805](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0805)

[Block Serial COM](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0805)

Ensure devices have an alternative method for communicating in the event that a valid COM port is unavailable.

ICS

[T0813](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0813)

[Denial of Control](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0813)

Provide operators with redundant, out-of-band communication to support monitoring and control of the operational processes, especially when recovering from a network outage[\[1\]](https://nvlpubs.nist.gov/nistpubs/SpecialPublications/NIST.SP.800-53r4.pdf). Out-of-band communication should utilize diverse systems and technologies to minimize common failure modes and vulnerabilities within the communications infrastructure. For example, wireless networks (e.g., 3G, 4G) can be used to provide diverse and redundant delivery of data.

ICS

[T0815](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0815)

[Denial of View](https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T0815)

Provide operators with redundant, out-of-band communication to support monitoring and control of the operational processes, especially when recovering from a network outage[\[1\]](https://nvlpubs.nist.gov/nistpubs/SpecialPublications/NIST.SP.800-53r4.pdf). Out-of-band communication should utilize diverse systems and technologies to minimize common failure modes and vulnerabilities within the communications infrastructure. For example, wireless networks (e.g., 3G, 4G) can be used to provide diverse and redundant delivery of data.

ICS
